<dsc reserve="468" >An optional single character-set modifier of an external method declaration, which governs the character set used to marshal strings during a call to the external method. The Unicode modifier marshals all strings to Unicode values, the Ansi modifier marshals all strings to ANSI values, and the Auto modifier marshals the strings according to COM+ rules based on the name of the method, or the alias name if specified. If no modifier is specified, the default is Ansi.</dsc>
